===== StepA4Criancas.jsx =====
// components/memorial/steps/StepA4Criancas.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES = [
    {
      valor: 'sim',
      label: 'Sim',
      subtexto: 'Várias crianças presentes',
      icone: 'baby',
    },
    {
      valor: 'nao',
      label: 'Não',
      subtexto: 'Apenas adultos',
      icone: 'x',
    },
    {
      valor: 'alguns',
      label: 'Alguns',
      subtexto: 'Poucas crianças',
      icone: 'users',
    },
];

export default function StepA4Criancas({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.criancas;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="Terão crianças na festa?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Crianças na festa
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Terão crianças na festa?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={opcao.valor}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('criancas', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,

===== StepA5Padrinhos.jsx =====
// components/memorial/steps/StepA5Padrinhos.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES_PADRINHOS = [
  {
    valor: true,
    label: 'Sim, já escolhemos',
    subtexto: 'Temos padrinhos definidos',
    icone: 'users',
  },
  {
    valor: false,
    label: 'Ainda não',
    subtexto: 'Vamos definir depois',
    icone: 'clock',
  },
];

export default function StepA5Padrinhos({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [escolhidos, setEscolhidos] = useState(estadoAtual?.padrinhosEscolhidos ?? null);
  const [quantos, setQuantos] = useState(estadoAtual?.quantosPadrinhos || '');

  const handleSelecionar = (valor) => {
    setEscolhidos(valor);
    if (!valor) {
      // Se não tem padrinhos, confirma imediatamente
      onSelect('padrinhosEscolhidos', false);
    }
  };

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    if (escolhidos === true && quantos !== '') {
      onSelect('padrinhosEscolhidos', true);
      onSelect('quantosPadrinhos', Number(quantos));
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Padrinhos
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Já escolheram os padrinhos?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES_PADRINHOS.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = escolhidos === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <Card
              key={String(opcao.valor)}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleSelecionar(opcao.valor)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  handleSelecionar(opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {escolhidos === true && (
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-3)', animation: 'fadeInUp 200ms ease-out' }}>
          <label style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
            Quantos padrinhos?
          </label>
          <input
            type="number"
            min="1"
            max="20"
            value={quantos}
            onChange={(e) => setQuantos(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Ex: 6"
            style={{
              padding: 'var(--space-3)',
              borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--color-border)',
              fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
              fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)',
              color: 'var(--color-text-primary)',
              background: 'var(--color-white)',
              maxWidth: '200px',
            }}
          />
        </div>
      )}

      {escolhidos === true && (
        <button
          aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
          disabled={quantos === ''}
          style={{
            alignSelf: 'flex-start',
            padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
            borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
            border: 'none',
            backgroundColor: quantos !== '' ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
            color: 'var(--color-white)',
            fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
            fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
            fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
            cursor: quantos !== '' ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
          }}
        >
          Confirmar
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

StepA5Padrinhos.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepA5Padrinhos };


===== StepA6DataPrevista.jsx =====
// components/memorial/steps/StepA6DataPrevista.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';

export default function StepA6DataPrevista({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.dataPrevista || '');

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    if (valor) {
      onSelect('dataPrevista', valor);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Data prevista
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Qual mês/ano aproximado?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <input
          type="month"
          value={valor}
          onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)}
          style={{
            padding: 'var(--space-3)',
            borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
            border: '1.5px solid var(--color-border)',
            fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
            fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)',
            color: 'var(--color-text-primary)',
            background: 'var(--color-white)',
          }}
        />
        <button
          aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
          disabled={!valor}
          style={{
            alignSelf: 'flex-start',
            padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
            borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
            border: 'none',
            backgroundColor: valor ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
            color: 'var(--color-white)',
            fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
            fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
            fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
            cursor: valor ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
          }}
        >
          Confirmar
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepA6DataPrevista.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepA6DataPrevista };


===== StepA7TempoJuntos.jsx =====
// StepA7TempoJuntos — Há quanto tempo estão juntos?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Input

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Input from '../../ui/Input';

export default function StepA7TempoJuntos({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.tempoJuntos || '');

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    onSelect('tempoJuntos', valor.trim());
  };

  const podeAvancar = valor.trim().length > 0;

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '480px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-5)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Há quanto tempo estão juntos?
      </h1>
      <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)' }}>
        Conte-nos um pouco da história de vocês.
      </p>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <Input label="Tempo juntos" value={valor} onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ex: 3 anos, 8 meses"  />
      </div>

      <button
        aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
        disabled={!podeAvancar}
        style={{
          alignSelf: 'flex-start',
          padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
          borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
          border: 'none',
          backgroundColor: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
          color: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-white)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
          fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
          fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
          fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
          cursor: podeAvancar ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
        }}
      >
        Confirmar
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

===== StepA8MoramJuntos.jsx =====
// StepA8MoramJuntos — Já moram juntos?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Já dividimos o mesmo lar" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Ainda moramos separados" }
];

export default function StepA8MoramJuntos({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.moramJuntos;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Moram juntos" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Já moram juntos?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepA8MoramJuntos.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepA8MoramJuntos };

      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );

// StepB14AgendouCartorio — Já agendou no cartório?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Já agendei a data no cartório" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Ainda não agendei" }
];

export default function StepB14AgendouCartorio({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.agendouCartorio;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Agendamento no cartório" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Já agendou no cartório?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>

      </div>

===== StepB16DefiniramEntrada.jsx =====
import { getTermos } from "../../../utils/linguagemCasal";
// StepB16DefiniramEntrada — {`Já definiu a entrada de ${termos.pessoa1} e ${termos.pessoa2}?`}
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Input

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Input from '../../ui/Input';

export default function StepB16DefiniramEntrada({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const perfil = estadoAtual?.perfilCasal || "nao-especificar";
  const termos = getTermos(perfil);
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.definiramEntrada || '');

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    onSelect('definiramEntrada', valor.trim());
  };

  const podeAvancar = valor.trim().length > 0;

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '480px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-5)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        {`Já definiu a entrada de ${termos.pessoa1} e ${termos.pessoa2}?`}
      </h1>
      <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)' }}>
        Descreva como será a entrada (opcional).
      </p>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <Input label="Entrada" value={valor} onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)} placeholder={`Ex: ${termos.pessoa1} com o pai, ${termos.pessoa2} já no altar`}  />
      </div>

      <button
        aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
        disabled={!podeAvancar}
        style={{
          alignSelf: 'flex-start',
          padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
          borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
          border: 'none',
          backgroundColor: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
          color: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-white)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
          fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
          fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
          fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
          cursor: podeAvancar ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
        }}
      >
        Confirmar
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

StepB16DefiniramEntrada.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepB16DefiniramEntrada };

// components/memorial/steps/StepB5CriancasCerimonia.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES = [
    {
      valor: true,
      label: 'Sim',
      subtexto: 'Daminhas, pajens, porta-alianças',
      icone: 'baby',
    },
    {
      valor: false,
      label: 'Não',
      subtexto: 'Cerimônia apenas com adultos',
      icone: 'x',
    },
];

export default function StepB5CriancasCerimonia({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.criancasCerimonia;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="Terão crianças na cerimônia?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Crianças na cerimônia
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Terão crianças na cerimônia?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={String(opcao.valor)}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('criancasCerimonia', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepB5CriancasCerimonia.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"

        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',

        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Duração da cerimônia
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Quanto tempo dura a cerimônia?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={opcao.valor}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('duracaoCerimonia', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}

                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>

  );
})}
      </div>

// StepC12ConvidadosForaCidade — Quantos convidados são de fora da cidade?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Input

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Input from '../../ui/Input';

export default function StepC12ConvidadosForaCidade({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.convidadosForaCidade || '');

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    onSelect('convidadosForaCidade', valor.trim());
  };

  const podeAvancar = valor.trim().length > 0;

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '480px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-5)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Quantos convidados são de fora da cidade?
      </h1>
      <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)' }}>
        Isso ajuda a planejar hospedagem e transporte.
      </p>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <Input label="Número" value={valor} onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ex: 15"  />
      </div>

      <button
        aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
        disabled={!podeAvancar}
        style={{
          alignSelf: 'flex-start',
          padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
          borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
          border: 'none',
          backgroundColor: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
          color: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-white)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
          fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
          fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
          fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
          cursor: podeAvancar ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
        }}
      >
        Confirmar
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

StepC12ConvidadosForaCidade.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepC12ConvidadosForaCidade };


===== StepC13HotelIndicacao.jsx =====
// StepC13HotelIndicacao — Precisam de indicação de hotel?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Queremos indicar hotéis para os convidados" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Não precisamos de indicação" }
];

export default function StepC13HotelIndicacao({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.hotelIndicacao;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Indicação de hotel" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Precisam de indicação de hotel?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepC13HotelIndicacao.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepC13HotelIndicacao };

// components/memorial/steps/StepC4Estacionamento.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';

import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES = [
    {
      valor: 'sim',
      label: 'Sim',
      subtexto: 'Estacionamento disponível no local',
      icone: 'car',
    },
    {
      valor: 'nao',
      label: 'Não',
      subtexto: 'Sem estacionamento próprio',
      icone: 'x',
    },
    {
      valor: 'valet',
      label: 'Valet',
      subtexto: 'Serviço de manobrista',
      icone: 'user',
    },
];

export default function StepC4Estacionamento({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.estacionamento;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="Como será o estacionamento?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Estacionamento
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Como será o estacionamento?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;

        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={opcao.valor}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('estacionamento', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{

                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

===== StepC6CapacidadeLocal.jsx =====
// components/memorial/steps/StepC6CapacidadeLocal.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';

export default function StepC6CapacidadeLocal({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.capacidadeLocal || '');

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    if (valor !== '') {
      onSelect('capacidadeLocal', Number(valor));
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Capacidade do local
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Qual a capacidade do local?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <input
          type="number"
          min="0"
          value={valor}
          onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Digite um número..."
          style={{
            padding: 'var(--space-3)',
            borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
            border: '1.5px solid var(--color-border)',
            fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
            fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)',
            color: 'var(--color-text-primary)',
            background: 'var(--color-white)',
          }}
        />
        <button
          aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
          disabled={valor === ''}
          style={{
            alignSelf: 'flex-start',
            padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
            borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
            border: 'none',
            backgroundColor: valor !== '' ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
            color: 'var(--color-white)',
            fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
            fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
            fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
            cursor: valor !== '' ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
          }}
        >
          Confirmar
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepC6CapacidadeLocal.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepC6CapacidadeLocal };


===== StepC7GeradorLocal.jsx =====
// components/memorial/steps/StepC7GeradorLocal.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES = [
    {
      valor: 'sim',
      label: 'Sim',
      subtexto: 'Gerador próprio disponível',
      icone: 'zap',
    },
    {
      valor: 'nao',
      label: 'Não',
      subtexto: 'Precisaremos contratar',
      icone: 'x',
    },
    {
      valor: 'nao_sei',
      label: 'Não sei',
      subtexto: 'Precisamos verificar',
      icone: 'help',
    },
];

export default function StepC7GeradorLocal({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.geradorLocal;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="O local tem gerador?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Gerador
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          O local tem gerador?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={opcao.valor}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('geradorLocal', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepC7GeradorLocal.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepC7GeradorLocal };

// StepD11TrajeNoivoContratado — {`Já contratou traje do ${termos.pessoa2}?`}
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import { getTermos } from '../../../utils/linguagemCasal';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Já tenho alfaiate/loja" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Ainda não contratei" }
];

export default function StepD11TrajeNoivoContratado({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);
  const perfil = estadoAtual?.perfilCasal || 'nao-especificar';
  const termos = getTermos(perfil);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.trajeNoivoContratado;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label={`Traje do ${termos.pessoa2} contratado`} style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

        {`Já contratou traje do ${termos.pessoa2}?`}
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>

// StepD13TransporteContratado — Já contratou transporte?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Já tenho carros/ônibus reservados" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Ainda não contratei" }

    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);

    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {

    }
  };
  return (

  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Já tenho fotógrafo" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Ainda não contratei" }
];

export default function StepD4FotografoContratado({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.fotografoContratado;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Fotógrafo contratado" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Já contratou fotógrafo?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepD4FotografoContratado.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepD4FotografoContratado };

===== StepE10QuemPaga.jsx =====
// StepE10QuemPaga — Quem está pagando o {termos.celebracao}?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import { getTermos } from '../../../utils/linguagemCasal';

export default function StepE10QuemPaga({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);
  const perfil = estadoAtual?.perfilCasal || 'nao-especificar';
  const termos = getTermos(perfil);

  const OPCOES = [
    { valor: "noivos", label: `${termos.pessoa1} e ${termos.pessoa2}`, desc: `Nós pagamos tudo` },
    { valor: "pais_noiva", label: `Pais do ${termos.pessoa1}`, desc: `Família do ${termos.pessoa1} assume` },
    { valor: "pais_noivo", label: `Pais do ${termos.pessoa2}`, desc: `Família do ${termos.pessoa2} assume` },
    { valor: "ambos_pais", label: "Ambos os pais", desc: "As duas famílias dividem" },
    { valor: "outros", label: "Outros", desc: "Outra combinação" }
  ];

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.quemPaga;

  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Quem paga o evento" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Quem está pagando o evento?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

===== StepE11FormaPagamento.jsx =====
// StepE11FormaPagamento — Qual a forma de pagamento preferida?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "pix", label: "PIX", desc: "Transferência instantânea" },
  { valor: "boleto", label: "Boleto", desc: "Pagamento parcelado" },
  { valor: "cartao", label: "Cartão", desc: "Crédito ou débito" },
  { valor: "transferencia", label: "Transferência", desc: "TED/DOC entre contas" }
];

export default function StepE11FormaPagamento({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.formaPagamento;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Forma de pagamento preferida" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Qual a forma de pagamento preferida?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

StepE11FormaPagamento.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepE11FormaPagamento };

===== StepE13HorarioMakingOfNoiva.jsx =====
// StepE13HorarioMakingOfNoiva — Horário do making of da {termos.pessoa1}
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Input

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Input from '../../ui/Input';
import { getTermos } from '../../../utils/linguagemCasal';

export default function StepE13HorarioMakingOfNoiva({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [valor, setValor] = useState(estadoAtual?.horarioMakingOfNoiva || '');
  const perfil = estadoAtual?.perfilCasal || 'nao-especificar';
  const termos = getTermos(perfil);

  const handleConfirmar = () => {
    onSelect('horarioMakingOfNoiva', valor.trim());
  };

  const podeAvancar = valor.trim().length > 0;

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: '480px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-5)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Horário do making of da 
      </h1>
      <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)' }}>
        Que horas começa a preparação?
      </p>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        <Input label="Horário" value={valor} onChange={(e) => setValor(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ex: 10:00" required />
      </div>

      <button
        aria-label="Confirmar resposta" onClick={handleConfirmar}
        disabled={!podeAvancar}
        style={{
          alignSelf: 'flex-start',
          padding: 'var(--space-3) var(--space-6)',
          borderRadius: 'var(--radius-md)',
          border: 'none',
          backgroundColor: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-border)',
          color: podeAvancar ? 'var(--color-white)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
          fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)',
          fontSize: 'var(--text-base)',
          fontWeight: 'var(--font-medium)',
          cursor: podeAvancar ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',
        }}
      >
        Confirmar
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

StepE13HorarioMakingOfNoiva.propTypes = {
  onSelect: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  estadoAtual: PropTypes.object,
};

export { StepE13HorarioMakingOfNoiva };

import React, { useState } from 'react';

  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Visto já emitido ou não necessário" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Preciso agendar ou solicitar" }
];

export default function StepE18Visto({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {

  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {

      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Visto para destino" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>

      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',

      }}
    >

===== StepE19Vacinas.jsx =====
// StepE19Vacinas — Vacinas da lua de mel em dia?
// Dependências diretas: React, PropTypes, Card

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';

const OPCOES = [
  { valor: "sim", label: "Sim", desc: "Cartão de vacina atualizado" },
  { valor: "nao", label: "Não", desc: "Preciso verificar ou tomar vacinas" }
];

export default function StepE19Vacinas({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.vacinas;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Vacinas da lua de mel" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Vacinas da lua de mel em dia?
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

    }
  };
  return (

    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div role="radiogroup" aria-label="Escolha uma opção" style={{ maxWidth: '640px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-6)', animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out' }}>
      <style jsx>{`@keyframes fadeInUp { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }`}</style>

      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>
        Certidão de óbito
      </h1>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fit, minmax(160px, 1fr))', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card key={opcao.valor} interactive selected={isSelected} padding="lg" onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)} role="radio" aria-checked={isSelected} tabIndex={0} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); handleCardClick(opcao); } }}>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
                <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)' }}>{opcao.label}</span>
                {o.desc && <span style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-muted)' }}>{o.desc}</span>}
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// components/memorial/steps/StepG10MenuInfantil.jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Card from '../../ui/Card';
import Icon from '../../ui/Icon';

const OPCOES = [
    {
      valor: true,
      label: 'Sim',
      subtexto: 'Opções kid-friendly no buffet',
      icone: 'baby',
    },
    {
      valor: false,
      label: 'Não',
      subtexto: 'Crianças comem o mesmo menu',
      icone: 'x',
    },
];

export default function StepG10MenuInfantil({ onSelect, estadoAtual }) {
  const [cardPulsando, setCardPulsando] = React.useState(null);

  const selecionado = estadoAtual?.menuInfantil;


  const handleCardClick = (opcao) => {
    if (cardPulsando) return;
    setCardPulsando(opcao.valor);
    setTimeout(() => {
      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="Terão menu especial para crianças?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Menu infantil
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Terão menu especial para crianças?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={String(opcao.valor)}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('menuInfantil', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

      onSelect(opcao.campo || opcao.valor, opcao.valor, opcao.cor);
      setCardPulsando(null);
    }, 350);
  };
  const handleKeyDown = (e, opcao) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleCardClick(opcao);
    }
  };
  return (
    <div
      role="radiogroup"
      aria-label="Como será o controle de bebidas?"
      style={{
        maxWidth: '640px',
        margin: '0 auto',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        gap: 'var(--space-6)',
        animation: 'fadeInUp 300ms ease-out',
      }}
    >
      <style jsx>{`
        @keyframes fadeInUp {
          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        }
      `}</style>

      <div>
        <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-display)', fontSize: 'var(--text-3xl)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-tight)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-2)' }}>
          Bebidas por pessoa
        </h1>
        <p style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
          Como será o controle de bebidas?
        </p>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(1, 1fr)', gap: 'var(--space-4)' }}>
        {OPCOES.map((opcao) => {
          const isSelected = selecionado === opcao.valor;
          return (
            <div
      key={opcao.valor}
      style={{
        transition: 'transform 300ms ease, box-shadow 300ms ease',
        transform: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? 'scale(1.03)' : 'scale(1)',
        boxShadow: cardPulsando === opcao.valor ? `0 0 0 3px ${opcao.cor || 'var(--color-brand)'}` : 'none',
        borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
      }}
    >
      <Card
              key={opcao.valor}
              interactive
              selected={isSelected}
              padding="lg"
              onClick={() => handleCardClick(opcao)}
              role="radio"
              aria-checked={isSelected}
              tabIndex={0}
              onKeyDown={(e) => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  onSelect('bebidasPorPessoa', opcao.valor);
                }
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 'var(--space-3)' }}>
                <div style={{
                  width: '48px',
                  height: '48px',
                  borderRadius: 'var(--radius-lg)',
                  backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand-lighter)' : 'var(--color-surface)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: isSelected ? 'var(--color-brand)' : 'var(--color-text-muted)',
                  flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <Icon name={opcao.icone} size={24} ariaHidden={true} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-lg)', fontWeight: 'var(--font-semibold)', color: 'var(--color-text-primary)', marginBottom: 'var(--space-1)' }}>
                    {opcao.label}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', fontSize: 'var(--text-sm)', color: 'var(--color-text-secondary)', lineHeight: 'var(--leading-relaxed)' }}>
                    {opcao.subtexto}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Card>
    </div>
  );
})}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
